 History of Meerut Lok Sabha seat Meerut, the city that laid the foundation of the freedom struggle in 1857, is considered the center of politics of western Uttar Pradesh
 desh main hue pehle loksabhaa chunaav main yahaan congress kaa paracham laharaaya, lekin 1967 main socialist party ne congress ko maat di
 In 1971, the Congress won again, but in its next election, the wave against Emergency went in favor of Janata Party
 haalanki, 1980, 1984 main congress kii ore se mohasina kidawai or 1989 main janata party ne ye seat jiti
 The Ram Temple movement in the country in the 1990s saw a direct impact in Meerut and after this the seat became the stronghold of the Bharatiya Janata Party
 1991, 1996 or phir 1998 main yahaan se lagaataar bhartiya janata party ke dabang netaa amarpal singh ne jeet darj kii
 After that in 1999, 2004, Congress and BSP respectively won from here
 haalanki, 2009 or 2014 main phir yahaan bhartiya janata party kaa paracham laharaaya

 angreji ke model varb Can or Could kaa prayog bolte or likhte samay kaaphi kiya jaataa he
 It is important to know the rules so that it is used in the correct place in the sentence frame
 jaaniye kahaan hota he Can or Could kaa prayog or in donon main kya fark he?1
 When there is a possibility of something, (a) Can we use Present Tense
 philhal kya sambhav ho saktaa he iske liye Can kaa prayog kiya jaataa he
 Example: You can easily walk in moonlight
 (b)vahiin, Could kaa prayog Past tense ke liye hota he
 Example: You could easily walk in Moonlight
 (c)could kaa prayog bhavishya ke liye bhi kiya jaataa he lekin yah nishchit nahin hota
 Example: If you don't hurry you could be late
 (yahaan der ho bhi sakati he or nahin bhi)2
 If we want to give or give permission to someone, (a) we use Can to get permission to do some work from someone
 example:can i do this job, please?you Can go home now if you like
 (b) However, in such a situation it would be better to use Could because it shows your civility
 example:could i do this Work, please?you Could go your home3
 For request and instructions (a) If we seek help from anyone or ask us to do some work, then we also use Can
 example:can i use your Phone, please?can i have my Water Bill, Please?(b)madad maangate vakt ham Could kaa prayog karen to yah zyada behatar hoga
 Starting such sentences with Could will tell your good behavior
 example:could i use Your Phone, please?could i have my Water Bill, Please?4
 (A) Can is used to describe one's skills to indicate aptitude
 example:she can sing a classical Song
 (b) At the same time, Could is used to explain one's past in terms of eligibility
 example:he Could run like a leopardshe Could Sing a Classical song
 5
 kuch ofer karnaa ho tokisi ko kuch ofer karne ke liye ham Can kaa prayog kar sakate hai
 Example: Can i do this if You like? jananath ke daravaajon ko taaja rang-rogan kii darkaar he
